<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_30d4b5f0-4741-4a6a-8eb1-ceeb599d9ad1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText14740024638334714757" style="display:none">Hanna Boudreaux has lived in the small town of Willow all her life. She’s sweet, cute and quiet. <br /><br />Hanna has a moment of epiphany when she realizes her crush for forever, Raiden Ulysses Miller, is not ever going to be hers. She sees her life as narrow and decides to do something about it. <br /><br />Raiden Miller is the town’s local hero. A former Marine with the medal to prove his hero status, he comes home, shrouded in mystery. It takes a while, but eventually Hanna catches his eye. <br /><br />After all these years of Raid and Hanna living in the same town, the question is why? Is Raid interested in Hanna because she’s sweet and cute? Or does Raid have something else going on?</span>

          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>  </div>

<div id="bookReviews">
  




  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_510474825" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510474825" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510474825?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510474825" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16461621322165008892"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405768i/790960._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>(My casting for Raid ^^)<br/><br/>4.5 stars<br/><br/><i> <b> ‘Cause all you gotta know is, it’s gonna be you and only you until the day I die… You’re not just enough for me. You’re everything I want.” </b></i> <br/><br/>The Queen of Alpha Males strikes again!<br/><br/>Ohhhhh the ANTICIPATION of starting a Kristen Ashley book!! Its like Christmas and birthday all rolled into one. I saw there for a good several minutes with my heart pounding just starting at the first page. Starting a KA book gives me the same feeling as jumping off a diving board – </span>
  <span id="freeText16461621322165008892" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405768i/790960._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(My casting for Raid ^^)<br><br>4.5 stars<br><br><i> <b> ‘Cause all you gotta know is, it’s gonna be you and only you until the day I die… You’re not just enough for me. You’re everything I want.” </b></i> <br><br>The Queen of Alpha Males strikes again!<br><br>Ohhhhh the ANTICIPATION of starting a Kristen Ashley book!! Its like Christmas and birthday all rolled into one. I saw there for a good several minutes with my heart pounding just starting at the first page. Starting a KA book gives me the same feeling as jumping off a diving board – its exciting, thrilling, and you just KNOW that once you jump, there’s no turning back…<br><br>And I jumped.<br><br>I loved Raid, loved Hanna, loved their dynamic together, love the writing style (but of COURSE). But I will say this – and its not a complaint, just an observation – this book felt a little “muted” compared to some of KA’s other reads (and I’ve read all but 5 of them). Again, this isn’t a bad thing, but it just seemed be muted in every respect – like a photo that has been slightly desaturated. There were all the elements that we all LOVE and adore and live for in a KA book, but at the same time, they were just a little… muted.<br><br>Raiden “RAID” Miller is a man’s man – tall, muscular, gorrrrrrgeous – and Hanna has been in love with him ever since she first met him. He was nine. Unfortunately, he never seemed to notice her and despite being utterly gone for him by the time they were in high school, they lived in their separate worlds and still, he didn’t notice her. After high school, he went straight off to become a badass Marine and no one had really seen him since. Until he came back.<br><br>Fifteen years later, after most of his squad was tragically killed, Raid returnes to the town of Willow — a hero responsible for saving the lives of everyone from his squad who survived… and this time, Hanna catches his eye.<br><br>A few dates, much flirting and some misunderstandings later and the sparks begin to flyyyyy!!<br><br>First of all, I seriously can’t even TELL you how much KA’s writing affects me. All she has to do is write the word “badass” and my heart flutters. Make that “badass Marine” and I’m pretty much just reduced to a hyperventilating pile of goo. Add chin lifts to the equation and seriously, my heart just melts. A badass Marine doing a chin life to his girl = **MAJOR HEART FLUTTERS**<br><br>Raiden — what can I say, I’m in love with him. Here’s your visual: think tall, muscular, cargo pants, tight tee, aviators pushed back into his thick dark hair, gorgeous green eyes and a deep sexy voice. Add that to his uber Alpha male protectiveness and a seriously BOSSY and self assured attitude and … **MELT**<br><br><i> <b> “Whether you got that in your bed before you go or hope to find it when you get back, that’s why you do it. You do it for her. You do it to keep her safe…. You get home in one piece, she’s your reward.”<br><br>His body pressed into mine…<br><br>“You’re my reward, Hanna.” </b></i> <br><br>I loved Hanna too! She had a wonderful voice – the beginning of the story was told in her POV and her voice was fun, sassy and totally relatable in many ways. She was an open book – cute and goofy and lovable.<br><br>It was a shorter KA book than most of them – maybe even the shortest one that I have (judging by those little dots on my Kindle). At first I have to say that it didn’t really feel like it fit in with the Unfinished Hero “feel” of the series, but there is more to the story than meets the eye. You get little hints of it here and there. Its a subtle feeling. And when it all comes out, coinciding with a switch to Raid’s POV, that’s when you start seeing more of the Unfinished Hero feel begin.<br><br>When the secrets come out, Hanna is thrown right into his world. Raid doesn’t hold back and doesn’t keep secrets from her. He is upfront and honest – expecting her trust, but also giving it.<br><br>This book was smoking HOT! Like I said, Raid was bossy. Demanding. Controlling in the bedroom. But… he never pushed her. He was ALL about equal enjoyment. He tried out a few things that were beyond her (and my) comfort zone but the moment he sensed her uncertainty, it was off the menu. I loved that about him. But yeah… bossy! <br><br><i> “Right now, its just you and me.”<br>“Okay, Raiden.”<br>“And you’re not leaving.”<br>My belly flipped.<br>“Okay,” I breathed. </i><br><br><i> <b> “I need you to trust it all to me.”<br>I was again confused. “Trust all what to you?”<br>“This,” his hands slid up my ribs and tightened. “You. All of you. I want you to trust it all to me.” </b></i> <br><br>Seriously – KA just “gets” interactions. Dynamics. To the core. There is something just so RIGHT about them. Her words – everything – has WEIGHT. Depth. Just hits you right in the heart ♥<br><br>I loved that Raid did have a few epic screw ups but he also had epic apologies (I love a man who can say sorry!!). The thing about KA guys is that they always have some weird logic to their crazy actions… lol, its Alpha male logic. But I loved that he wouldn’t let anything get between them. He screwed up once but after that he wasn’t going to let anything get in their way.<br><br><i> “I give you shit, you do not eat it. Like today, you give it back to me. We’ll work it out, Hanna.” </i> <br><br>This book had me squeeing out loud, grinning and fanning myself! There’s this huge feeling of being torn between wanting to read every world as slowly as you can to make it last and reading as fast as you can to just get more more more. It was very character focused. There’s less action in this story that most KA books and no actual bad guy. I’m really going with the term “slightly muted” on it though. I found it a little slow in certain parts and I didn’t connect “quite” as strongly to it as I did to some of the other KA books but I did still love it. I loved being in the KA world, I loved revisiting some of the characters (yes, Knight and Creed have cameos!) and I loved meeting yet another gorgeous, swoony Alpha to add to my book boyfriends list.<br><br>Overall I give it 4.5 stars.<br><br>*** I'm adding in a note here regarding reading order because a LOT of you have been asking about it. Hmmm I'm a HUGE stickler for reading books in order, especially KA books. But, technically you *can* read this one alone... however, both Knight and Creed have cameos in this book and it would actually be better if you could read them all in order. Plus there's the fact that CREED was actually my favorite one of the series and if you're going to read Creed, then you really should read Knight first cuz stuff from Knight plays into Creed... so yeah... just read them in order if you can :)<br><br>See above for my Casting photo for RAID :)<br><br>For more of my reviews, come visit my book blog at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/">http://aestasbookblog.com/</a><br>Or come join my group <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16461621322165008892" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510224405" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510224405?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510224405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4941296485898220117"><b>4 FEEL–GOOD Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Let's face it–Kristen Ashley writes romance like no other!</b><br/><br/>What a great book! In this story, Kristen Ashley gives us a solid, admirable hero and two amazing 5 star characters in Hanna, the heroine, and her great-grandmother, Miss Mildred. How I loved this amazing great-grandmother. She's the shining star of the story. Hanna is now my all-time favorite Kristen Ashley heroine. She's everything I love in a strong female lead. She's simply divine! As for the epilogue...well...it's on</span>
  <span id="freeText4941296485898220117" style="display:none"><b>4 FEEL–GOOD Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Let's face it–Kristen Ashley writes romance like no other!</b><br /><br />What a great book! In this story, Kristen Ashley gives us a solid, admirable hero and two amazing 5 star characters in Hanna, the heroine, and her great-grandmother, Miss Mildred. How I loved this amazing great-grandmother. She's the shining star of the story. Hanna is now my all-time favorite Kristen Ashley heroine. She's everything I love in a strong female lead. She's simply divine! As for the epilogue...well...it's one of Kristen Ashley's best, and that's saying something. <br /><br />There's always a scene or two in each of Kristen Ashley's books that seems to sum up the couple for me. In Raid, this was the scene. I just loved it! I read it again and again. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>She stared into his eyes and announce, “A good-bye kiss.” It was at that Raid stopped dead. “What?”<br /><br />“Raiden, the gig is up,” she declared and Raid closed his eyes.<br /><br />Jesus, how could the woman be so infuriating and so fucking cute all at once?<br /><br />He opened his eyes and asked, “The gig is up?”<br /><br />She leaned into him and hissed, “Yes.”<br /><br />Fuck, he wanted to kiss her.<br /><br />He also wanted to shake her.<br /><br />“Baby, it’s the jig,” he corrected and her head jerked which made the mess of hair on her head jerk, which reminded him he wanted his hands in that hair.<br /><br />Then elsewhere.<br /><br />He needed to speed this shit up.<br /><br />“Sorry?” she asked, sounding confused and he looked from her hair to her eyes and saw she was, in fact, confused.<br /><br />Yeah. Infuriating. And fucking cute.<br /><br />“The jig is up, not the gig,” he told her.<br /><br />Her eyes narrowed. “Seriously? You’re correcting my street lingo?<br /><br />“Think that street lingo was the street lingo about eight decades ago, Hanna. So now it’s just lingo.”<br /><br />Hanna threw up her hands. “Now you’re giving me a street lingo history lesson?”</b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><i>ARC kindly provided to <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a> by Kristen Ashley and Chas in exchange for an honest review</i><br /><br />-----<br />If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</span>

  <span id="freeText2569878266108980215" style="display:none"><b>buddy read with Jamie and girls on 28th!!!!!</b><br /><br />ok this is my first KA review! <div id="review_510215338" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510215338" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510215338?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-kristen-ashley">author-kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=reviewed-for-author">reviewed-for-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=sexy-deliciousness">sexy-deliciousness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-must-read">series-must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-unfinished-heroes">series-unfinished-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=military-ex-military">military-ex-military</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-ebook">format-ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510215338" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16875352718903589497"><br/><br/><i>
  <b>5 hot, exciting, romantic stars!</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Raid</i> is the third book in Kristen Ashley’s Unfinished Hero series and right from the start, grabbed hold and never let go. It’s sweet, it’s funny, it’s sexy... yep! It’s all kinds of awesome!<blockquote><b>Description...</b><br/><br/>Hanna Boudreaux has lived in the small town of Willow, Colorado all her life. The great-granddaughter of the town matriarch, she's sweet, cute and quiet.<br/><br/>Too quiet.<br/><br/>Hanna has a moment of epiphany when she realizes her crush for forever, Raiden Ulysses Miller, i</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16875352718903589497" style="display:none"><br /><br /><i>
  <b>5 hot, exciting, romantic stars!</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>Raid</i> is the third book in Kristen Ashley’s Unfinished Hero series and right from the start, grabbed hold and never let go. It’s sweet, it’s funny, it’s sexy... yep! It’s all kinds of awesome!<blockquote><b>Description...</b><br /><br />Hanna Boudreaux has lived in the small town of Willow, Colorado all her life. The great-granddaughter of the town matriarch, she's sweet, cute and quiet.<br /><br />Too quiet.<br /><br />Hanna has a moment of epiphany when she realizes her crush for forever, Raiden Ulysses Miller, is not ever going to be hers. She sees her life as narrow and decides to do something about it.<br /><br />Raiden Miller is the town of Willow's local hero. An ex-marine with the medal to prove his hero status, he comes home, shrouded in mystery. It takes a while but, eventually, Hanna catches his eye.<br /><br />But after all these years of Raid and Hanna living in the same town, the question is, why? Is Raid interested in Hanna because she's sweet and cute? Or does Raid have something else going on?</blockquote><b>My review...</b><br /><br />If you’ve read the previous books in this series, Knight and Creed, you know that these “unfinished heroes” are men who don’t just walk the edge of honor, they spit on it, cross it, and never look back. They’re men who live and love by their own code, make no excuses for what they do, and Raiden Ulysses Miller is no different. And thank God for that!<br /><br /><i>Hanna. </i>She is such a doll! She’s cute, she’s funny, she’s clever and talented… she’s absolutely awesome. With her girlie girl bike, and girlie girl basket and cutsie handlebar streamers, she’s a woman who knows what she likes and isn’t embarrassed to flaunt it. She loves life and does everything she can to make sure the people around her love life, too. She’s the kind of person who is so amazing, so awesome, that if I can’t be her, I’d want to be part of her world. And that’d be true even if she wasn’t getting a <i>happily ever after</i> with one incredibly sexy man.<br /><br />Speaking of which…<br /><br /><i>Raid. </i>Intense. Solid. Honorable. Sexy. Devoted. Confident. He’s a man who knows that there’s a big gray area between what’s right and what’s wrong, and I love how he works that area to his advantage. In truth, the world needs more men like Raiden Ulysses Miller. I think of all KA’s unfinished heroes - not just those in the series - he’s the most grounded, and the most okay with what he does, which is something else I love about him.<br /><br />There’s something extra special about this story, and it's Hanna's great grandmother, Miss Mildred, who is an absolute hoot! I don't think I've ever enjoyed a 'secondary' character as much as I enjoyed her, and truth be told, there's nothing 'secondary' about her. Everything about this woman shines, and I absolutely adore her! Between Raid, Hanna and Miss Mildred, the first several chapters of this story put such a huge smile on my face that my cheeks hurt, seriously! And then as the story continues, the people and places of Willow, Colorado kept that smile there, and, had me laughing, sighing, fanning myself and sobbing so hard I couldn’t see to keep reading… and I loved each and every minute of it.<br /><br /><b>The bottom line...</b><br /><br />What can I say? Raid’s a typical Kristen Ashley hero, but there’s something… <i>more</i>… about him... something that makes him stand out from the others. He’s truly incredible and I love how he gives Hanna the <i>happily ever after</i> she's always dreamed of. And Hanna, with her rose colored glasses and beautiful spirit – I love how she gave Raid the <i>happily ever after</i> that he not only needs, but one he's more than deserving of.<br /><br /><i>They are, each to the other, their reward.</i><br /><br /><i>My thanks to Kristen Ashley and Chas for providing Blithely Bookish Reviews with a copy of Raid in exchange for an honest review! What a HUGE treat this has been! </i><br /><br />Follow Kristen Ashley on <a href="http://m.facebook.com/pages/Kristen-Ashley/83283039199?id=83283039199&amp;refsrc=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.com%2Fsearch&amp;_rdr" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> and <a href="http://twitter.com/#!/KristenAshley68" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a><br /><br />-----<br />If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16875352718903589497" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer530768070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16490168150759140248">For an awesome Kristen Ashley Giveaway, pop over to <a href='http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2013/02/blog-tour-giveaway-review-raid-by.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a>!<br/><br/><a href='http://beta.photobucket.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786785i/487612.png' alt=' photo raidsreward_zpsfc341d65.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It’s been a while since I’ve been in the loving arms of a Kristen Ashley alpha hero and it’s so nice to be back – it kind of feels like coming home. When I first discovered Kristen Ashely, I read her books slavishly but, now, I have to wait for new releases and I was so excited and honoured to received an ARC of Raid and I’m delighted to report that it’s another classic Kristen Ashley – compelling, romantic and se</span>
  <span id="freeText16490168150759140248" style="display:none">For an awesome Kristen Ashley Giveaway, pop over to <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2013/02/blog-tour-giveaway-review-raid-by.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a>!<br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786785i/487612.png" alt=" photo raidsreward_zpsfc341d65.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It’s been a while since I’ve been in the loving arms of a Kristen Ashley alpha hero and it’s so nice to be back – it kind of feels like coming home. When I first discovered Kristen Ashely, I read her books slavishly but, now, I have to wait for new releases and I was so excited and honoured to received an ARC of Raid and I’m delighted to report that it’s another classic Kristen Ashley – compelling, romantic and sexy as hell!<br><br><br>Raiden Ulysses Miller, from now on known as Raid is our Unfinished Hero. He’s absolutely typical Kristen Ashley hero material – he’s bossy, he knows what he wants, he’s protective, he’s gorgeous and he’s burning white-hot for Hanna, our dorktastic heroine. Raid has had it tough it has to be said. After growing up with a violent, bullying father he joined the marines and lost most of his crew when an op went totally FUBAR in Afghanistan and has returned home and now works in the shady underworld headed up by Knight Sebring. When he looks at Hanna – he sees something that’s full of goodness, a complete contrast to his life so far and he sees her as his reward for a life lived hard.<br><br><br>Hanna, his reward, is our totally dorky, cute, sweet and very lovable heroine – think Meg Ryan or Sandra Bullock as gorgeous, loveable kooks in a chick flick and you have the measure of Hanna. She’s been crushing on Raid her whole life and he’s never once noticed her. Now he’s back from the Marines she’s hanging out at his sister’s cafe in the hope that he will see her until she sees me him making out with a woman who couldn’t be more different than her. Losing hope, she gives up and decides this is a turning point and that she must go live her life to the full as Raid is never going to be hers. She hardly ever saw Raid but, unknown to her, he had started to notice her.<br><br><br>So, Raid pursues Hanna and she can’t believe her luck but questions his motives and we start along the tortuous angsty path that you’ll be familiar with if you’re a Kristen Ashley fan. Raid is just a little bit kinky and likes to play and Hanna finds that she’s really not as vanilla as she thought as they practically set fire to my Kindle with their steamy sex scenes. Oh yes, I enjoyed these!! Raid, of course, is fiercely protective of Hanna – she’s like a ray of sunshine brightening up his dark, troubled world and the Raid that came back from Afghanistan is not the same man that went but, slowly, Hanna is putting that smile back on his face and helping him heal and face up to his nightmares. Raid, right from the beginning, knows that Hanna is the one that he wants but can he keep her protected and hidden from the shady world he inhabits?<br><br><br>A big shout out must go to the scene stealing pair of Miss Mildred, Hanna’s great-grandmother and Spot, her very ornery cat. Miss Mildred may now be sitting in her porch chair in the sunset of her life but she’s a fiercely protective old matriarch and sees straight away that Raid is perfect for Hanna but also sees the fire burning inside and warns Hanna to be prepared. She’s not a woman used to holding back her opinions and I laughed frequently at her antics and also at Spot, ankle slasher extra-ordinaire! Hanna also has a best friend that you will recognise if you’re a die-hard Kristen Ashley fan.<br><br><br>I did think Raiden was a pretty unusual name and had to giggle at the following scene……..<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Raiden is a silly-ass romance novel hero’s name my Mom came up with to torture me,” he <br>replied. <br>I stifled a giggle and remarked, “And Raid isn’t silly?” <br>He smiled. “Raid’s a badass’s name.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>OK Raid – you sure are a badass so we’ll let you get away with that one but that made me laugh!!<br><br><br>This is a great continuation of the Unfinished Hero series and we get to catch up with Knight, Anya, Creed, Sylvie and Deacon – I sure hope Deacon gets his story some time very soon. I loved every second I was with this book – it’s funny, its very sexy, it’s sweet and romantic and there were a few gasp out loud moments and I even cried a little too and it’s pretty much all kinds of awesome! It’s just about perfect contemporary erotic romance. Kristen Ashley, really at her finest.<br><br><br>4.5 stars erotic romance<br><br><i>ARC courtesy of Kristen Ashley &amp; Chas with thanks </i><br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8150235885975908041"><br/><b>ALL HAIL KRISTEN ASHLEY, QUEEN OF ALPHA MALES!</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/456710.gif' width='500' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Kristen, you are killing me... Every damn time! I've reached a point that I measure all the men in my life using your "scale". I want a boyfriend/man that will back me up against a wall, call me a loveable and ridiculous nickname, knock my socks off in and out of bed and order me around while I'm replying: "Alright, honey" and do whatever the hell I want... <br/><br/><blockquote><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405723ra/790826.gif' width='250' height='170' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></blockquote>

  <span id="freeText8150235885975908041" style="display:none"><br><b>ALL HAIL KRISTEN ASHLEY, QUEEN OF ALPHA MALES!</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/456710.gif" width="500" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Kristen, you are killing me... Every damn time! I've reached a point that I measure all the men in my life using your "scale". I want a boyfriend/man that will back me up against a wall, call me a loveable and ridiculous nickname, knock my socks off in and out of bed and order me around while I'm replying: "Alright, honey" and do whatever the hell I want... <br><br><blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405723ra/790826.gif" width="250" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>
<br><br>You are <b>ABSOFUCKINGMAZING</b> and you have us hooked.</i><br><br><b>4 Stars</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>“My reward.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405723i/790827.jpg" width="400" height="195" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is no exception in the general Kristen Ashley rule of awesomeness. Love, emotion, dynamics and interactions are fiercely realistic, you live with these heroes. And when you reach the end you feel like you lost your best friend...<br><br>Hanna Boudreaux has lived in Willow her whole life. The great-granddaughter of the town's matriarch she is respected and beloved. She is kind and generous and she is nursing the biggest crush EVER!<br><br><b>
  <i>“I fell in love with you when I was six and I didn’t know who you were.”</i>
</b><br><br>It's adorable and hilarious watching her trying to act cool and unaffected and you can't help but root for her..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405723ra/790828.gif" width="500" height="344" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She is easily one of the most relatable female leads. You respect her and you get her. She speaks her mind, doesn't take bullshit and deals with matters head on. Okay, her job creating afghans seems a little unbelievable but adds to her character making her more quirky and sassy.<br><br>But when her crush finally notices her, will she be able to tame the storm and survive the flames?<br><br><b>
  <i>“Raiden Ulysses Miller.”</i>
</b><br><br>An amazing name for an amazing man. Following the tradition of all KA males, he is obsessed, protective and possessive. But he hides some deep scars..<br><br>Raid, is also one of Willow's beloved children. He grew up in town taking care of his mother and sister, compensating for his deadbeat father. He joined the Marines and fought in Afghanistan but hasn't returned the same.. He left pieces of his soul behind and nightmares are haunting his nights. And what he chose for a living? It will take a strong woman to deal with all of these. Raid needs love...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405723ra/790829.gif" width="500" height="241" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two are finally on the same page and things are explosive. <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405723ra/790830.gif" width="250" height="141" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>Yes, hot and imaginative and heartwarming and sweet and amazing!<br><br>Hanna and Raid found the other half of their souls and will do anything to keep it. Fight demons, enemies and their own instincts...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405723ra/790831.gif" width="500" height="382" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>A special mention for Hanna's great-grandmother, Mildred... Her calmness, wisdom and acceptance ruled this book. Hilarious and outspoken as only a really old person can be, a reminder that grandparents deserve respect and unconditional love. <br><i>And that reminds me: Gran Virginia, my parents didn't name me after you as you wished, but that hasn't stopped you from adoring me... The feelings are mutual! ❤ Promise me you will live forever! ❤ (and now I hear your voice:"Don't be silly, child... Death is a whole new challenge and you know your grandfather is helpless up there without me..")❤ *sniff*</i></b> <br><br>My only wish/regret is that this book wasn't longer... I really wanted more interaction, more back-story, especially what happened to Raid, more EVERYTHING!<br><br>And a final warning... the epilogue destroyed me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391734ra/754264.gif" width="500" height="262" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>If you haven't read a Kristen Ashley book yet, you are really missing out...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/563733.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/535416224?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kinky">kinky</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer535416224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3589997953976241814"><b>Reading Raid - 5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Listening to Raid - 1 Star...and I may never recover from that horrible experience.</b><br/><br/>****<br/><br/>So I persevered until the very end and I have to say that the audio pretty much ruined my Raid experience. My rating will stay at 5 stars for the read...but I'm tempted to read it again just to cleanse me from that nightmare. <br/><br/>That bloody audio, the narrator butchered poor Raid's voice. Hannah's wasn't much better, but at least it was appropriate. There is nothing worse than listening to a</span>
  <span id="freeText3589997953976241814" style="display:none"><b>Reading Raid - 5 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Listening to Raid - 1 Star...and I may never recover from that horrible experience.</b><br /><br />****<br /><br />So I persevered until the very end and I have to say that the audio pretty much ruined my Raid experience. My rating will stay at 5 stars for the read...but I'm tempted to read it again just to cleanse me from that nightmare. <br /><br />That bloody audio, the narrator butchered poor Raid's voice. Hannah's wasn't much better, but at least it was appropriate. There is nothing worse than listening to a sex scene when it all sounds the same. When the moaning and the dirty talk sounds like the same person...it's kind of like...talking dirty to yourself?? I'm probably not explaining it well, but it kind of sounded like I was listening to a lesbian couple. No offence, but it's just not my cup of tea. His sexy demands really sounded bad in a woman's voice. I'm still pulling funny faces from the memory, even as I'm typing this review.<br /><br />Do yourself a favour, if you're thinking of trying out Raid - DO NOT EXPERIMENT WITH THE AUDIO. It has the potential to scar you for life (shudders).<br /><br />GUESS WHAT?? Wildest Dreams is downloading as I type!!! YAY!!!!<br /><br />*************************************<br />Oh my Lordy, I have loved every KA audio I've listened to so far, but this one is not going so well. The narrator can't change her voice to a male to save herself. I'm seriously struggling to differentiate between Hannah and Raid...and that's bad. I always pictured Raid with a deep and gravely voice, not the high pitched one I'm getting (shudders).<br /><br />I will persevere...<br /><br />After all, this is only to tide me over until WILDEST DREAMS comes out :-)</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer534670580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16765880955551114146"><b> 5 ‘Absofuckingmazing’ Stars!!!!! </b><br/><br/>Let me introduce you to my new favorite KA couple...<br/><br/><b>Raiden Ulysses Miller</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f1f199c1-a53c-42a7-97c4-0e7d0b564f4f_zpsef7d8387.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Hanna Boudreaux has had a crush on Raiden Miller since she has been six years old. She is now in her late twenties. She lives in the house she grew up in, is the town sweetheart, and helps take care of her ninety eight year old great grams.   <span id="freeText16765880955551114146" style="display:none"><b> 5 ‘Absofuckingmazing’ Stars!!!!! </b><br><br>Let me introduce you to my new favorite KA couple...<br><br><b>Raiden Ulysses Miller</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f1f199c1-a53c-42a7-97c4-0e7d0b564f4f_zpsef7d8387.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409426i/801675.jpg" alt=" photo f1f199c1-a53c-42a7-97c4-0e7d0b564f4f_zpsef7d8387.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> Hanna Boudreaux </b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/1467cbf4-01a6-4ed1-b3b6-2c7c4249149e_zps6ac88cea.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409426i/801676.jpg" alt=" photo 1467cbf4-01a6-4ed1-b3b6-2c7c4249149e_zps6ac88cea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Hanna Boudreaux has had a crush on Raiden Miller since she has been six years old. She is now in her late twenties. She lives in the house she grew up in, is the town sweetheart, and helps take care of her ninety eight year old great grams. She owns her own business, and spends most of her free time reading, watching movies etc. Not the most exciting life. <br>Raiden has been in the marines, after going to war, he is now home. Hanna spends months trying to catch Raid’s eye, but it never happens. She decides she needs a change. She wants to live a little. Have some fun, make some changes. She does all this, and Raid starts to notice.<br><br>Hanna was a near perfect heroine for me. She was funny, sweet, lovable and a bit of a dork.<br><b>I was a klutz and a dork. I was a dorky klutz!</b><br>I just loved her to pieces. <br>Raiden... oh Raid. In the words of Miss. Mildred... <b>
  <i>“He’s the cat’s pajamas.”</i>
</b><br>Raid is hot! He is an alpha male, of corse, sexy and protective. He has some issues, as do most who have been in war and seen the things he has seen, but he tries to work through them.<br><br>Raid goes after Hanna. He wants her to be his woman. She is flabbergasted. The man she has wanted for over twenty years finally wants her. It takes her a little time to get used to this.<br><b>
  <i>“You might want to try to stop being so sexy and hot and cool or you’ll give me a heart attack and then your plans for later will be completely derailed.”</i>
</b><br><br>Their relationship is not obstacle free. Raid’s job is complicated and seems a little sketchy at times. But Hanna has been in love with Raid forever, and he is starting to fall for her too. <br><b>
  <i>“Christ, no joke, it hurts to even look at you and believe you’re real. So fuckin’ sweet, I remembered there’s a God and He actually likes me.”</i>
</b> <br><br>Hanna and Raid have chemistry. Kristen Ashley can write a sex scene like no other... I was not disappointed with Raid!<br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/ce1dcf12-e89f-44d4-a4a0-372e8b98f67b_zpsede41568.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409426i/801677.jpg" alt=" photo ce1dcf12-e89f-44d4-a4a0-372e8b98f67b_zpsede41568.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“You’re gonna let me play with that body. You’re gonna let me work you ‘til you’re so fuckin’ wet you’re drenched for me. And when I let you come I’m gonna make it feel like you’re coming apart at the seams.”</i>
</b><br><br>Hanna and Raid are great together, but Raid has demons he is dealing with from his past, Hanna tries to help him, to fix him, but will she get burned?<br><b>A handsome man.<br>A damaged man.<br>A man I intended to fix.</b><br><br>I love everything I’ve read by Kristen Ashley, but her Unfinished Hero’s series is my favorite by far. Although Knight is still my favorite KA alpha man, Raid was a close second. And he and Hanna are most definitely my favorite KA couple. Raid is an awesome badass alpha and Hanna was great, someone you could see your self being best friends with. And I just loved her Gran. It was also great to see Sylvie, Creed, Anya, and Knight(swoooon). A fantastic story with a lot of love, sex, humor, smiles, drama and even a few tears. No KA book would be complete without a perfect ending/epilogue! A really great read I couldn’t put it down! <br><br>Some of my favorite lines:<br><br><i>
  <b>“Honey, you look straight out of a chick flick. Cute outfit. Glass of wine. Sexy, messy hair. Cute house that looks out of a magazine. Not a lick of makeup and you look prettier than any woman I’ve seen in over a year. Gabbin’ on the phone like you look this good, in a place that looks this good every day when that shit’s impossible. Chick flick.”<br><br>“How the fuck can you make something that makes no sense make sense?”<br><br>  “You, just like that, any man would fight and die for the privilege of comin’ home to that every day.”<br><br>“Now, are you gonna fuck me or spend the next hour talkin’ to me?” he asked.<br>“I suppose I’ll fuck you.” I muttered</b>
</i><br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/a0d51826-f198-4ee6-9a7a-35affe60b6fb_zps8c525be5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409426i/801678.jpg" alt=" photo a0d51826-f198-4ee6-9a7a-35affe60b6fb_zps8c525be5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9876620560022502906"><b> WHY KIT? WHY????????? Why that ending? No, you didn't spoil us with all your wonderful HEA... Can we go back to that? Please???</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405707ra/790756.gif' width='500' height='281' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>As you can see I am not a happy camper and I was the self appointed mayor of all that is KA shoving it down into everyone's throat to read (in a nice way of course)... but this... this! I did not expect. That ending alone almost erased all the hotness that was before. <br/><br/><br/>So to deal with this I am developing an amnesia... and the story OFFICIALLY ended Pre-Prologue... THERE</span>
  <span id="freeText9876620560022502906" style="display:none"><b> WHY KIT? WHY????????? Why that ending? No, you didn't spoil us with all your wonderful HEA... Can we go back to that? Please???</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405707ra/790756.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As you can see I am not a happy camper and I was the self appointed mayor of all that is KA shoving it down into everyone's throat to read (in a nice way of course)... but this... this! I did not expect. That ending alone almost erased all the hotness that was before. <br><br><br>So to deal with this I am developing an amnesia... and the story OFFICIALLY ended Pre-Prologue... THERE! so much better... now on to the review.<br><br><br><b>
  <u>MEET MY RAID!</u>
</b><br><br><div>
  <a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/489133209498870632/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411340142i/11217179._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><div>
  <p>

    <a href="http://pinterest.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>
  </p>
</div><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br><br>Hanna is a typical mousey homebody girl who has had a crush on Raiden since she was 6. Now all grown up she sits in his sister's cafe waiting to catch a glimpse of him... but he never does... until she transforms. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405707ra/790758.gif" width="500" height="467" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And honestly she doesn't even pop up on his radar because of her attitude and clothes transformation... oh no! she gets on pop-up on his WORK RADAR first.<br><br>So obviously in his macho ways he goes about getting a date with her by being pushy and well all macho till her brain melts 'till she's just barely coherent enough to nod her response. <b>H-O-T!</b><br><br>But he more than noticed her then... she becomes his <b>REWARD</b>.<br>As an ex-marine he has his demons. Demons that Hanna sets up to battle. Helping him through his nightmares with some "bumps" in the road but she accomplishes does it with love and care and long legs and Betty Sue look and shitload of patience.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I waited for you for almost a lifetime. I’m not going to get you and have any of the good parts torn away, like you sleeping somewhere else. I like sleeping with you. I feel safe with you beside me. I wake up happy. They don’t get to take that from me, and further, they don’t get it from you.” <br>He gave me a light shake. <br>“Babe, tonight, no clue what I was doin’, I threw you across the room.” “Throw me out the window, I don’t care. Just don’t make me sleep without you.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><div>
  <a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/489133209498980831/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411340105i/11217174._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="249" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><div>
  <p>

</div><br><br>Other than that ending... this is classic KA... feel good romance, hot sex, crazy town &amp; it's inhabitants, wacky family, HOT SEX, bitchy ex, ornary animal, danger, oh and have I mentioned HOT SEX?<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You good?” <br>“Um… they haven’t measured this level of good, thus it has as yet gone undefined, so the answer is yes, but the word is wrong.” <br>His arms tightened and his body started shaking. Idiotically, I kept talking. <br>“I’ll be contacting Webster tomorrow. My suggestion will be absofuckingmazing.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>KA certainly exploring different kinky sexual life-styles in this one and I applaud her. Might not be my thing but she is a strong advocate to "If it doesn't work for you, speak up! Both parties should enjoy it"<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Suddenly, he asked, “Trust me?” <br>“Yes,” I answered immediately. <br>“Then on all fours, baby, crawl to me and do it slowly.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Personally I should have listened to everyone else and NOT read the Epilogue and this book would have been a solid 5 for me. But alas...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405707i/790760.jpg" width="499" height="333" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Special Thank you to all my buddy Reads on this Book: Jamie, Sultan, Jamie, Jillian, Allison, Sharon, Vishous, AnnMarie, Carla, Cheryl, Heather, Tammy and I hope I didn't forget anyone else... you made the thread so entertaining and hilarious. We have to do it AGAIN... soon!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405707i/790761.jpg" width="500" height="332" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405707ra/790762.gif" width="420" height="178" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7334184538427861840">I loved Knight <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13565914-knight'>https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1...</a> , Creed <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13640229-creed'>https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1...</a> , so-so. <br/>Raid is the 3rd book in Kristen Ashley’s Unfinished Heroes Series and I enjoyed it immensely….one of the reasons being the heroine’s grandmother. She was such a fabulous and unforgettable character……<blockquote>
  <b>“Don’t get ideas. That boy’s behind won’t mount a bike, precious. He might blow one up in a military exercise, but he’s not gonna ride alongside you while you mosey into town and pick </b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7334184538427861840" style="display:none">I loved Knight <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13565914-knight">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1...</a> , Creed <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13640229-creed">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1...</a> , so-so. <br>Raid is the 3rd book in Kristen Ashley’s Unfinished Heroes Series and I enjoyed it immensely….one of the reasons being the heroine’s grandmother. She was such a fabulous and unforgettable character……<blockquote>
  <b>“Don’t get ideas. That boy’s behind won’t mount a bike, precious. He might blow one up in a military exercise, but he’s not gonna ride alongside you while you mosey into town and pick up salad fixin’s for dinner.”</b>
</blockquote> <br>Raiden Ulysses Miller,<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413900158i/11578527.jpg" alt=" photo b495c482cc86349f5390831551ac0662_zpsf3fb08e8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">ex Marine hero comes back home, trying to deal with PTSD and the darkness of his time in service meets Hanna Boudreaux,<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413900158i/11578528.jpg" alt=" photo d6a2e28135266ce105ea54c260b36d0b_zps48754861.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">the sweet and lovely local girl, who has had a crush on Raid since she was 6 years old….he of course, has never noticed her.<br>Hanna decides she needs to change her life….new look, sporty new car, soon gets her noticed……<br>There are some dark moments and some really hilarious ones…..the dialogue had me rolling on the floor a few times.<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413900158i/11578529.jpg" alt=" photo 9fadc3a15197311f27b7e5931f4169d3_zps187bd371.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>Loved seeing these two finding and healing each other…… a true HEA…..<blockquote><b>“Cause all you gotta know is, it’s gonna be you and only you until the day I die… You’re not just enough for me. You’re everything I want.” </b></blockquote> Next one…Deacon, the bounty hunter!!!!!</span>

  <i>delicious</i>
</b>. Hanna is sweet, real, and very likable. The big surprise was Hanna's scene stealing adorable and worldly Great Gram & her cat Spot!! Nobody does swoon worthy hot uber alpha males like Kristen Ashley and Raid is no exception. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/f01de435f53692ce01d3b316bdc8c7f2_zps33ed32fd.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Hanna fell in love with Raid when she played tug of war on his team when she was 6 yrs old. Twenty plus years lat</span>
  <span id="freeText1613098695231186712" style="display:none"><b>Another <i>FanFreakinTastic</i> 5 Star KA Read!!!!</b><br><br>This is best and my favorite (so far...) in KA's "Unfinished Hero" series. Raiden Ulysses Miller is <b>
  <i>delicious</i>
</b>. Hanna is sweet, real, and very likable. The big surprise was Hanna's scene stealing adorable and worldly Great Gram &amp; her cat Spot!! Nobody does swoon worthy hot uber alpha males like Kristen Ashley and Raid is no exception. <br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/f01de435f53692ce01d3b316bdc8c7f2_zps33ed32fd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Hanna fell in love with Raid when she played tug of war on his team when she was 6 yrs old. Twenty plus years later, when Raid returns home after leaving the Marine's Hanna does what she can to catch his eye. When she spots him with a skanky skank she gives up hope figuring since she's not a skank, she doesn't stand a chance at him noticing her.<br><br> <a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/albums/z369/dshewey1/?action=view&amp;current=ec0cf5eef8ef46b34a48a5f88b829eb5_zpsc598f198.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <b>“If you’re the kind of woman who can withstand the blaze of hellfire he’s got burning inside, he battles that and wins, you will know nothing for the rest of your life, no taste, no experience, not even the birth of your children that will be sweeter than the love he’ll have for you.”- Mrs. Mildred, (Gram)<b></b></b>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1062589211" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062589211" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062589211?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062589211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer247627469789876740"><b>4 porch swings and sweet rewards STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415474093i/11795847.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If you’re the kind of woman who can withstand the blaze of hellfire he’s got burning inside, he battles that and wins, you will know nothing for the rest of your life, no taste, no experience, not even the birth of your children that will be sweeter than the love he’ll have for you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Oh man, that was all kinds of sweet and adorable and naughty and heartbreaking and a little cheesy...but in a good way...I think. ;D<br/><br/>Book number three in the <i>Unfinish</i></span>
  <span id="freeText247627469789876740" style="display:none"><b>4 porch swings and sweet rewards STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415474093i/11795847.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If you’re the kind of woman who can withstand the blaze of hellfire he’s got burning inside, he battles that and wins, you will know nothing for the rest of your life, no taste, no experience, not even the birth of your children that will be sweeter than the love he’ll have for you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh man, that was all kinds of sweet and adorable and naughty and heartbreaking and a little cheesy...but in a good way...I think. ;D<br><br>Book number three in the <i>Unfinished Hero</i> series and this time around we meet Raid and Hanna. A hard ass alpha-male, *duh* and a sweet country girl who couldn't be more different if they tried.<br><br>I'm sorry, it took me a while to write this review, just because in the meantime I read two other Kristen Ashley books and there is no end in sight. Suffice to say, I love Ms. Ashley and I love her domineering bad boys even more. Almost like a drug I can't quit. Freaking unbelievable. My sleeping time has gone down to 3-4 hours a night.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415727196ra/11835784.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Yup, that's how I feel about KA! No regrets.<br><br>But let's get to the good part. What's it all about and why you need to read this freaking series and most importantly why we all need to invest in a house with a swing on the porch.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I fell in love with you when I was six and I didn't know who you were.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>It all started years ago in a small town called Willow, Colorado. Little Miss Sunshine, also known as <b>Hanna Boudreaux</b>, develops a crush on Raid, the boy every girl in town loves and who indecently never even noticed our heroine. Doesn't stop her from daydreaming about him, but... Yup, life is hard and then you die...or something like that. ;P<br><br>Years later, Hanna lives her life looking after her ninety-seven year old great-grandmother and in her free time stalking the town’s favourite son, who -after serving in the Marines- went off the grid, just to reappear in Willow six months earlier.<br><br>I have to confess, I had a few problems with the first chapter. It basically was all about Hanna obsessing/borderline stalking Raid, it was annoying as hell and it got me worried for a sec. But there is a silver lining...it's just KA's way to set up the story and it's just one chapter. No need to panic.<br><br>Luckily after a little eye opener Hanna decides to pull it together and change her life. Oh boy, she does that. From one day to the other she expands her business, gets a make-over, buys a new car and oh, that new ridiculous bike she drives around town. Finally, as it turns out Hanna is actually a really nice heroine. She is sweet, caring, independent and whole lot of dorky and cute.<br><br>Funny thing is, the moment Hanna changes her life and focuses on actually living it the tables turn. Would you believe that Raid suddenly notices her? Well, there might be a twist, but I can tell you he is looking, and what he sees doesn't disappoint. Question is...WHY?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Honey, you look straight out of a chick flick. Cute outfit. Glass of wine. Sexy, messy hair. Cute house that looks out of a magazine. Not a lick of makeup and you look prettier than any woman I’ve seen in over a year. Gabbin’ on the phone like you look this good, in a place that looks this good every day when that shit’s impossible. Chick flick.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Raiden Ulysses Miller</b>, just like all the other unfinished heroes is a marvellous book-boyfriend. He is all kinds of sexy, incredibly good looking, territorial, bad-ass and so sweet with Hanna...*sigh* its heaven, right out of the KA hand-book.<br><br>But what is a perfect hero without the dark back-story and a little drama? Not much, right? So yeah, Raid has demons mostly pertaining to his past in the military, but he is working on it and it is possible that Hanna can help a little.<br><br>The thing I liked most about Raid is his determination, he knows what he wants and he is here to collect...beg, borrow or steel. No questions asked. He wants his 'reward' and he is out to get it. ;D<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You,that dress, those shoes, that hair, beverages and furniture you can get horizontal on would not be a good combination.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Contrary to the last book, this one wasn't as drawn out and littered with unnecessary plot repeats. Yes, in true KA fashion the book is a slow burner and highly detailed, but I didn't lose interest or felt the need to skip anything. <br><br>Raid and Hanna's story was sweet and very cheesy at times...but in a good way. In fact, I think within the <i>Unfinished Heroes</i> series this one is the most mellow and harmless book. But I still loved reading it. There is no point in writing 5 books which are all the same, so a change was quite welcome. <br><br>That is not to say that Raid is a soft character, quite the opposite. He is an anti-hero through and through. He has very little if any regard for the law and of course he works with Creed and Knight. That just tells you everything you need to know.<br><br>I really loved the side characters...especially Hanna's great-grandma, who has this almost clairvoyant look on things, but I guess that comes with age and having lived it all before. Also, honorary mentions for Raid's mum and sister.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415739991ra/11838586.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just one last thing and I'll be done...promise. Why are there 63 people who labelled this book with BDSM? Who are these vanilla people? Yes, they play a little, but seriously...that's just playing with my hopes. For those of you who read the kinky stuff a lot please don't expect anything too explicit.<br><br>The sex scenes are pretty HAWT and Raid sure is a on the alpha-male side of the spectrum, but honestly...it's all very tame.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I couldn’t stop myself from being the woman who tried to withstand hellfire. No. I knew the reason. It was because I wanted to know nothing for the rest of my life sweeter than the love Raiden could have for me. It was also more. I wanted him to know nothing for the rest of his sweeter than what I could give him.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Turns out I didn't have an answer to the porch question after all...oh well, read the book and find out. ;D<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer5709118319351046918"><i>Written April 27, 2015</i><br/><br/><b>4.2 Stars - A very sweet <i>sharing / giving / growling / mumbling / etc...</i> tender hot KA</b><br/><br/><i>Raid</i> is a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> book that has been waiting in my e-reader more than two years now. When I saw there was a newly published audiobook I cheered and downloaded it at onc. ~ Just three more bucks and hope of 9:30 hours well invested listening time. <br/><blockquote>“Babe, tell me right now you aren’t fuckin’ with me.”<br/>“I’m kind of fucking with you in the hopes that you’ll return the favour,” I replied.</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5709118319351046918" style="display:none"><i>Written April 27, 2015</i><br><br><b>4.2 Stars - A very sweet <i>sharing / giving / growling / mumbling / etc...</i> tender hot KA</b><br><br><i>Raid</i> is a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> book that has been waiting in my e-reader more than two years now. When I saw there was a newly published audiobook I cheered and downloaded it at onc. ~ Just three more bucks and hope of 9:30 hours well invested listening time. <br><blockquote>“Babe, tell me right now you aren’t fuckin’ with me.”<br>“I’m kind of fucking with you in the hopes that you’ll return the favour,” I replied.’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/e139eea9d7403e1f8d984ee613486a3f_zps4fbd7004.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430153745i/14687092.jpg" alt=" photo e139eea9d7403e1f8d984ee613486a3f_zps4fbd7004.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>Wisely invested coins, well spent listening-time</b><br>In my opinion a steamy romantic KA treat as done for a girl like me right now. Not too kinky (as book #1 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13565914.Knight__Unfinished_Hero___1_" title="Knight (Unfinished Hero, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Knight</a> partly was) for my "delicate" taste neither. <br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><i>Willow — a small town somewhere in Colorado</i><br><br><b>Hanna Boudreaux</b> is a sweet and nice small town girl at her twenty seven year. When she realizes her crush for forever, <b>Raiden Ulysses Miller</b>, is not ever going to be hers she start to change her life and her style. ...A tiny little bit. <br><br>Raid, a former Marine, is the town’s local war hero with the medal to prove his status. He came home, is quite mysterious, seems dangerous and first after a while catches the funny, blond and beautiful Hanna his eye. <br><br>...A touching but also sizzling hot romance story starts. Not "bang on" but maybe insta.<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Couple%20in%20love/7e7688db-65df-4259-ac9b-f58e3cdc582f_zpstyfosa7t.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426794705i/14097398.jpg" alt=" photo 7e7688db-65df-4259-ac9b-f58e3cdc582f_zpstyfosa7t.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“Downstairs, you made a decision,” he stated quietly, and my breath started to quicken. <br>He was very right. I did. I nodded. <br>“I know it freaked you, baby, but I hope you come to understand what I gave you downstairs was a gift that, in giving, means a fuckuva lot to me.”</blockquote><br>*********************************************************<br><br>There are a lot of 'sharing' and 'giving' just as a sweet KA romance should be. The hero is a growling alpha male dream, the heroine is cute and easy to like and these two are hot together. Add a very old witty grandma, a fat lazy cat and a short meeting with some favorite characters from other books. <br><blockquote>“You think I’m a man who’s got a thing that good, he’ll let it go?” <br>“No,” I whispered. <br>“That would be fuck no,” he corrected.’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/e139eea9d7403e1f8d984ee613486a3f_zps4fbd7004.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430153745i/14687092.jpg" alt=" photo e139eea9d7403e1f8d984ee613486a3f_zps4fbd7004.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“Did I just get surrounded by a pack of hot guys and a petite woman who is clearly badass who are all off to hunt my man, who’s off hunting the man that had three of his goons beat the dickens out of me?”</blockquote><br><b>The audiobook edition and narrator</b><br>Simply wonderful and pleasantly narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7123621.Dara_Rosenberg" title="Dara Rosenberg" rel="nofollow noopener">Dara Rosenberg</a> at its best. This shorter format is also kind of great if you don't have time for an ordinary much longer KA audiobook (usually 16 - 24 hours). <br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><i>Raid</i> felt really quick, light and easy —not much actually happens— but the lovestory, steam and grunting h@rny hero were there so it was in all ways pretty okay. <br>Highly recommended in this new audiobook shape as well.<br><br><b>I LIKE - yummy heart touching stories from Ms Ashley</b></span>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone; KA fans don't miss it!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer556634601" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1108884361089768433"><i>No synopsis here, just thoughts...</i><br/><br/>Well I give up. I finished this book over a week ago and still haven't written a review? And do you know why? Because I've run out of superlatives for this author. Every KA book that I've read has been a winner, but this one...Raid...and Hanna? I've just loved them so much...words escape me. I'm not even going to try anymore. <i>Everything</i> about this one worked for me--muscular, former Marine drop-dead-gorgeous alpha tough guy (but not over-the-top alpha like so ma</span>
  <span id="freeText1108884361089768433" style="display:none"><i>No synopsis here, just thoughts...</i><br><br>Well I give up. I finished this book over a week ago and still haven't written a review? And do you know why? Because I've run out of superlatives for this author. Every KA book that I've read has been a winner, but this one...Raid...and Hanna? I've just loved them so much...words escape me. I'm not even going to try anymore. <i>Everything</i> about this one worked for me--muscular, former Marine drop-dead-gorgeous alpha tough guy (but not over-the-top alpha like so many of KA's heroes) was <i>the</i> perfect alpha hero. He had issues, but they weren't insurmountable (at least nothing that a cute, nerdy, crushing-on-him-forever, afghan-making, lovable, relateable heroine can't fix), and he worked a little outside the law but "who cares?" I loved this gentleman Alpha! And I loved good girl Hanna and that spitfire great- grandma of hers! Oh yeah, and "Spot" the cat!:) 'Nuff said. Fans of KA (and fans of a good old erotic contemporary) do yourself a favor and <b>read this book</b>--you won't be sorry. It has everything--good story, awesome characters and character development, hot sex, fabulous epilogue...and just the right book length. This book grabbed me so much, I haven't picked up another one since (and I should really get it out of my system by now). This ranks right up there with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750.At_Peace__The__Burg___2_" title="At Peace (The 'Burg, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">At Peace</a>, and Raiden Miller is my favorite Kristen Ashley hero.. <b>5 big stars</b>!<br><br><i>Hanna...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/004_zps09a1cb34.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><i>Raid...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/raid1_zps23aeb1ef.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379788775i/514174._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo raid1_zps23aeb1ef.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
