    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_548554856" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548554856" />
    <a title="Shelley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7526630-shelley"><img alt="Shelley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370799427p2/7526630.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548554856?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelley" href="/user/show/7526630-shelley">Shelley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7526630-shelley?shelf=scarred-hero">scarred-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7526630-shelley?shelf=uber-alpha-male">uber-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7526630-shelley?shelf=lovable-heroine">lovable-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7526630-shelley?shelf=meh">meh</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548554856" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2573643615271596388">Sitting down with a KA novel you know what you are going to get, it’s agreed. <br/>For loyal fans everywhere KA books are a blanket of love, hope, optimism and (let’s be honest) wishful thinking. These books are for the girl in all of us who want to be wrapped up in the arms of a big strong handsome hunky hero (anti or not), finding, conquering and fixing the man, who is your soul mate who will love and adore YOU above all others no matter how fat your arse is.<br/> <br/>This is the perfect formula for romance</span>
  <span id="freeText2573643615271596388" style="display:none">Sitting down with a KA novel you know what you are going to get, it’s agreed. <br />For loyal fans everywhere KA books are a blanket of love, hope, optimism and (let’s be honest) wishful thinking. These books are for the girl in all of us who want to be wrapped up in the arms of a big strong handsome hunky hero (anti or not), finding, conquering and fixing the man, who is your soul mate who will love and adore YOU above all others no matter how fat your arse is.<br /> <br />This is the perfect formula for romance novels, and it works. Ms Ashley is the queen of the alpha man romance, giving her readers the confidence to believe in themselves as real woman and not feel the need to be skinny -minny plastic fantastic. Her message is we are woman, we work it and we rock what we got! <br /><br />In this I applaud you Kristen Ashley always and forever.<br /><br />So it is with a heavy heart that I fail to find the love for this book. As a loyal fan and consummate devourer of her books I can honestly say that her stories are beginning to fall flat. <br /><br />I have ignored all editorial issues, long running sentences, first person POV (a personal pet hate) monosyllabic dialogs, the over use of “and then… “ and “I know this because…” in the past purely because Ms Ashley can tell a tale so riveting and compelling with fabulous characters, action packed plots, heartfelt romance, steamy sex, humour and drop dead gorgeous alpha hero’s. I simply don’t care when the story is that great! But this is not that great, not at all.<br /><br /><i>Raid</i> offers only a sniff of what her other books have to offer. The relationship building is non-existent; it’s rushed and lacks any tension in anticipation. <br />The plot is vague in its direction and then the culmination is glossed over with a, it’s done comment which gives the reader no real insight as to what happened at all. I was bored, it has to be said.<br /><br />It is hard not to compare <i> Raid</i> to her previous books <i> At Peace, Sweet Dreams, Motorcycle Man, Mystery Man</i> (I could go on) where her plots are filled with anticipation and suspense, they are well rounded, fleshed out and provocative, sexy, fast paced and totally enthralling. <i> Raid </i> is none of these things. Nope, not even the sexy part. <br /><br />I feel it’s come to a point where her alpha males are all meshed into one. Raid could quite easily be Tack, Ty, Creed or any of the others in fact. Their dialog is the exactly same in every book, the way they think, the way they move, their rambling alpha speeches have the same tone and message, their seductions with words like “eyes on me”, “give me your mouth” <br />I have read it all before, they all say it, again and again. It’s all becoming just a little bit <i>too</i> familiar, which is okay (I guess, kind of… no not really) if the plot was something I could sink my teeth into and just get on with it. <br /> <br />I really do hope to see a return of the KA magic in her next books with a bit more originality, the same recipe of course but just more glimmer, and shine with some angst and suspense and a plot that has me guessing all the way through. This is easy stuff for her, she’s done it before;)<br /><br />They say great books ruin us for mediocre books. This is true.<br /><br />PS: The stars are for Grammy and Spot.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2573643615271596388" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4239604086199527564"><b> 3 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I was underwhelmed with this read. I always struggle with books that have the "I've loved you forever" theme, so that could be the reason. I love experiencing the development of feelings in these relationships, and because there was already those strong feelings for the h (who is our main POV) -- I missed all of that. It just made it so I didn't personally connect with the characters or their connection to each other (I hope that makes sense). I didn't hate it and I didn</span>
  <span id="freeText4239604086199527564" style="display:none"><b> 3 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I was underwhelmed with this read. I always struggle with books that have the "I've loved you forever" theme, so that could be the reason. I love experiencing the development of feelings in these relationships, and because there was already those strong feelings for the h (who is our main POV) -- I missed all of that. It just made it so I didn't personally connect with the characters or their connection to each other (I hope that makes sense). I didn't hate it and I didn't love it either...it was just ok.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Hanna and Raid's story. Hanna has been in love with Raid since she was 6 years old, but older Raid never even knew who she was. After she finally decides to move on from her unrequited crush, she starts to expand her simple life with making new friends and experiencing new things. Raid all of a sudden starts taking notice of her, and goes full on pursuit of her. They date and fall in love. There is some past baggage in their way, but after some work and sexy times ;)...they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Hanna (mostly) and Raid's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b>Ok. I found it too slow at times, and the ending was abrupt in the sense that I asked myself "that was it?". I never skimmed though.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of. They start with the h already having strong feelings for the H, and the H says that he fell in love with her at first sight (he says this later on, and didn't confess until later either).<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3 stars. Raid. He was ok. He was alpha hot, but he could also be a jerk.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3 stars. Hanna. She was ok. I wanted her to be tougher at times, but I also enjoyed her quirkiness.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate. I teared up a few times, but never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H pushes away at one point because he is upset about the h bring up his past. The H is the main pursuer in the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story. Mild D/s play.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes and no <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Condoms are used until the h gets on birth control. I don't remember any mention of previous practices or std statuses.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ A ex f-buddy of the H's shows up and causes some drama for the h and H. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Not really<br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Drug dealing (side character on page), criminal activity (H off page), and loss of a loved one (on page) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had a kind-of abrupt ending, but a good epilogue with a HEA.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> It was part of my scribed subscription.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17288837826656347507"><b>MINI ORGASM ALERT~~MINI ORGASM ALERT~~ MINI ORGASM ALERT</b><br/><br/><img height='319' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/511723.gif' width='465' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Right, sorry about that....on with the review.....<br/><br/>So before I begin I think it's only fair that I be totally honest with you. I am a <b>HUGE </b> KA fan, I've read everything she's every written and it <u>never</u> grows old for me. In fact I'd even go as far as saying she could probably recite the alphabet and throw in a few badass alphas and a feisty chick and I'd lap it up, that's how big a fan I am. <br/><br/>In fact this is pretty much me, reading a KA book;<br/><br/><img height='167' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/485369.gif' width='298' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>R</span>
  <span id="freeText17288837826656347507" style="display:none"><b>MINI ORGASM ALERT~~MINI ORGASM ALERT~~ MINI ORGASM ALERT</b><br><br><img height="319" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/511723.gif" width="465" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Right, sorry about that....on with the review.....<br><br>So before I begin I think it's only fair that I be totally honest with you. I am a <b>HUGE </b> KA fan, I've read everything she's every written and it <u>never</u> grows old for me. In fact I'd even go as far as saying she could probably recite the alphabet and throw in a few badass alphas and a feisty chick and I'd lap it up, that's how big a fan I am. <br><br>In fact this is pretty much me, reading a KA book;<br><br><img height="167" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/485369.gif" width="298" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reading is an escape for me. Its a time where i get to sit back and immerse myself in someone else's story. I love nothing more than a bad ass, bad boy with a heart of gold, one that has a deep, dark past and a potty mouth to go with it. <br><br><b>"Baby, you stare at my dick any longer, Miss Mildred’s gonna have to send out a search party.”… “I was staring at your hip muscles,” I corrected. “Whatever,” he muttered, his lips now smiling too, then louder, “just sayin’, anything in that vicinity, your eyes on it, it’ll get thoughts on its own.”</b><br><br>One who needs to beat back the demons within, in order to win the girl. Better still, an anti hero who is overly confident, infuriating, arrogant and bossy, yet can make me melt by the amazing words that come out of his mouth. <br><br><b>"You ignite for me, but more, you make me ignite for you. And no woman, not in my whole goddamned life, has made me ignite the way you do.” </b><br><br>Enter Raid.....a former marine, the towns local hero, and the man whom Hanna Boudreaux has been in love with since she was six years old. Only trouble is, Raid doesn't seem to even notice Hanna, well until one day she catches his eye. But like any great contemporary romance Raid has a deep dark past and its up to Hanna to decide whether she is able or willing to take on the fire that burns within him.<br><br><b>“If you’re the kind of woman who can withstand the blaze of hellfire he’s got burning inside, he battles that and wins, you will know nothing for the rest of your life, no taste, no experience, not even the birth of your children that will be sweeter than the love he’ll have for you.” </b><br><br>Kristen Ashley, for me, is an author who has this unique ability to get me to open a book, and suddenly I'm in a semi dream state......I'm totally hooked (and believe me when i say it takes a lot to engage and hold my attention!), I'm hooked on the characters and the story line, I can't seem to stop reading, and I do it with a shit eating grin on my face. <br><br>Raid is a signature Kristen Ashley hero, and as such, every time I thought of him I think I had a mini preliminary orgasm. I loved this story and as usual, after reading a KA story, I walk away with a happy heart, a huge smile on my face, and a huge desire to chase my husband straight to the bedroom......or in this case to a porch swing!!<br><br><img alt="image" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/469427.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>*oh and just in case you wondered, it's 4 stars and not 5, just because I wanted to read a little more kinky stuff......but then again I'm a perv so I always want to read more kink! </b><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/527005325?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Brandi by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer527005325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2971272069409334519"><b>
  <i>“You’re my reward, Hanna.”</i>
</b> <br/><br/>At 6 years old Hanna Boudreaux fell in love with 9 year old Raiden Miller. But he didn't notice her, for years. So even though they grew up in the same small town, they never really interacted. As the years pass, Hanna continues to crush on Raiden. Now, years later, he has returned home a hero, but he still doesn't notice Hanna. So, Hanna decides to let go of her dream, and makes some changes. And guess what...He notices her. This was a fun read, and pretty short c</span>
  <span id="freeText2971272069409334519" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“You’re my reward, Hanna.”</i>
</b> <br><br>At 6 years old Hanna Boudreaux fell in love with 9 year old Raiden Miller. But he didn't notice her, for years. So even though they grew up in the same small town, they never really interacted. As the years pass, Hanna continues to crush on Raiden. Now, years later, he has returned home a hero, but he still doesn't notice Hanna. So, Hanna decides to let go of her dream, and makes some changes. And guess what...He notices her. This was a fun read, and pretty short compared to most KA books. Was it typical KA? Yes. Did I enjoy it?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400518752ra/9684710.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Raid is the sexy, alpha male - dangerous, protective, and 'playful'. He's moody and scary at times but he is dealing with a traumatic past and some PTSD.<br><br><i>
  <b>"All you gotta know is it's gonna be you--and only you--until the day I die, because life did not lead me down the wrong path when I fell in love with a girl who had the sun shinning in her hair who would eventually not do it for me. You're not just enough for me. You're everything I want."</b>
</i><br><br>Hanna is sweet, shy, and a bit naive. I loved her relationship with her grandmother - these relationships pull at my heartstrings, making me miss my grandmother terribly. There is nothing in the world like a grandmother...Back to Hanna, she's a bit insecure, but she also stands up for herself. I really enjoyed her character. <br><br><i>
  <b>“I know, child. What do you think's keeping me on this earth? Not easy to let go that kind of love. That kind of love's got the power to hold you tethered to a world you should have left a long time ago.” </b>
</i><br><br>Overall another entertaining KA book. I really enjoyed this one, but would have loved to have more of Raid's POV. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2971272069409334519" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_510336134" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510336134" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510336134?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=i-m-gonna-be-in-the-minority">i-m-gonna-be-in-the-minority</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=on-going-series">on-going-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510336134" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18193321585255752721">God, the agony of writing this review.<br/><br/>I devoured Kristen Ashley's backlist one book after the other (nearly all of them) in a month's time and since reading my first book of hers <i>The Gamble</i> I haven't looked back. She's like chicken soup, you go to your KA favorite when you've been having a bad book slump to make all things right again. And she does a pretty good job doing it. I never underestimate the healing power of Alex and Feb or Max and Nina. <br/><br/>So understandably, any KA release for me is some</span>
  <span id="freeText18193321585255752721" style="display:none">God, the agony of writing this review.<br /><br />I devoured Kristen Ashley's backlist one book after the other (nearly all of them) in a month's time and since reading my first book of hers <i>The Gamble</i> I haven't looked back. She's like chicken soup, you go to your KA favorite when you've been having a bad book slump to make all things right again. And she does a pretty good job doing it. I never underestimate the healing power of Alex and Feb or Max and Nina. <br /><br />So understandably, any KA release for me is something to get palpitations over.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Am I gonna traumatize the fat cat if he sees me fuckin' you?"</i>
</b><br /><br />Sadly, that and the conversation between Hanna and KC (about the tacos), was as good as it got for me for this book. <br /><br />Honestly, among her work, I am not a fan of this series. The alpha heroes are too much to be believably real. And if you know the other heroes in the KA universe that's saying something. They callout sex positions WHILE having sex ('Spread!' 'Give me your eyes.'), they suddenly speak to the heroine in the third person, they find the strangest things attractive in their heroines… it's crazy. The non-good kind. <br /><br />This one, I feel, got more shortchanged because Raid and Hanna felt like an amalgam of all the other heroes and heroines in KA's books that I can't give them any of my love at all because they sound like they're poor imitations of the original characters (who gets my original recipe love). Hanna had a conversation with Anya (from Knight) somewhere in the end of the book and she said how Hanna will get used to how things are and I'm thinking, well that conversation will probably turn up in the next book with Hanna giving the same pep talk to the new chick on the block. Raid wasn't even given a deep enough character profile for me to overlook his flaws. What happened with his unit was so vague, my brain couldn't latch on and empathize.<br /><br />Even the proverbial skanks that get thrown out midway through sound a rehash of previous skanks ("hey isn't that the girl from *insert KA book here*"). Speaking of the skanks, I read the Author's Note at the end of this book and I totally respect and admire her stand and efforts to cut this message across her readers… but skinny people are people too, you know? Every woman deserve to have their own happy ever afters, regardless of their body type, yes, but that should go both ways (curvy and skinny). With how the skinny-minnie women get repeatedly typecasted in a majority of these books, it's starting to sound like a witch hunt. <br /><br />I'm beginning to worry if I'm starting to outgrow KA's bag of tricks, I hope for the sake of Ren and Ally, I have not. But I'm getting warier and more critical of her recent releases. Maybe it's me who have recalibrated my expectations based on the other books that I've read instead of the quality of the work taking a dip. <br /><br />I really hope so… it's hard to find a good bowl of chicken soup these days.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18193321585255752721" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer530316350" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2412694558363008135"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I told you I didn’t dream as a kid of bein’ a cop or an astronaut, but I gave a lot of thought to the woman I’d want in my bed. I grew older and gave more thought to that woman, but it was also about the woman I wanted in my life. And she was you. Then I met you. And now, every day I wake up I cannot believe my luck because you’re here.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>Hanna Boudreaux's had a crush on Raiden Ulysses Miller since she was six years old. He was nine at the time, and came to her great-grandmot</span>
  <span id="freeText2412694558363008135" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I told you I didn’t dream as a kid of bein’ a cop or an astronaut, but I gave a lot of thought to the woman I’d want in my bed. I grew older and gave more thought to that woman, but it was also about the woman I wanted in my life. And she was you. Then I met you. And now, every day I wake up I cannot believe my luck because you’re here.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Hanna Boudreaux's had a crush on Raiden Ulysses Miller since she was six years old. He was nine at the time, and came to her great-grandmother's annual picnic. He was also beautiful. Twenty two years later, he's even more beautiful - and Hanna's still waiting for him to notice her. But, a lot of things happened in the meantime. The boy Hanna fell in love with is now a man. Ex-marine, with a lot of baggage, and a lot of mystery surrounding him. What she doesn't know is Raiden noticed her just when she accepted the fact she'll never have him, and decided to turn her narrow life upside down.<br /><br />Months later, <i>GI Joe</i>, and the girl that looks <i>straight out of a chick flick</i>, finally have a date. And, yes, this is one of those 'expect trouble immediately' kind of things. And, yes, this is also one of the reasons I absolutely adore Raid. He's gonna come out and say it - whatever it is he wants to say. Hell, he'll even pick a lock, so he can come <i>in</i> and say it. But, he will definitely not allow anything to stop him from finally claiming his reward. Because that's the most important thing of all. That's the reason to fight. That's the reason to survive it all. His reward. Hanna.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Now, I can share what came before you, and I had fun, Hanna. I make no apologies. But I think it’s best we leave it where it lies. ‘Cause all you gotta know is it’s gonna be you—and only you—until the day I die, because life did not lead me down the wrong path when I fell in love with a girl who had the sun shining in her hair who would eventually not do it for me. You’re not just enough for me. You’re everything I want. So that works for me.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br />I probably don't even have to mention the fact there were times when Raid managed to make me so mad I could scream - in many ways, he's a typical KA macho, alpha, bossy, badass guy. He's gonna say (and do) some seriously shitty things. But, when the good times come - when he's talking, sharing, and rocking your world over and over again - honestly, there's nothing sweeter than that.<br />Raid is quite straightforward. He reminds me of Knight - he even has that kinky/slightly dominant side. Nothing OTT, just enough to make a girl (me) happy. He's also got that anti-hero quality, that I've come to appreciate. What I'm trying to say is - <i>strictly speaking</i>, he's a criminal. Not that I'd care...<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You good?”<br />“Um… they haven’t measured this level of good thus it has as yet gone undefined so the answer is yes but the word is wrong.”<br />His arms tightened and his body started shaking.<br />Idiotically, I kept talking. “I’ll be contacting Webster tomorrow. My suggestion will be absofuckingmazing.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br />Hanna is such a sweet, lovely, goofy girl. In a way, she's perfect for Raid. Actually, they are perfect for each other. After all those years of crushing on him, she got her guy because she was brave enough to play with fire, and risk her heart along the way. She reminds me of Lexie, and that can never, ever be a bad thing. All the goofy/sweet things aside, Hanna is smart, and extremely devoted to her loved ones - Spot (the fat cat) included.<br />Which brings me to another favorite character of mine here - Miss Mildred, Hanna's great-grandmother. I wish I had someone just like her by my side, to push me when needed, to tell the stories of her life, and to show me how to enjoy every single day. We all need Miss Mildred. We should at least <i>try</i> to be like her. This world would definitely be a better place that way.<br /><br />So, <i>Raid</i> is (yet another) awesome KA story. It's got it all - alpha, badass hero, lovely heroine, amazing side characters, <i>hot</i> scenes, great dialogues, and a wonderful HEA. Everything you could possibly need is right there. And, after months of not having a new KA book to lose myself in, I've missed it a lot, and hoped Raid will be enough to keep me going (though re-reading does help a bit). I only wish it were (much, much) longer, as it seems way too short for my taste. Still, it packs quite a punch, and I'm glad I got to enjoy this story, meet another awesome guy, see some of my favorite characters once again, and laugh/sigh/giggle/drool for hours.<br /><br />If you've somehow managed to miss <i>Unfinished Hero</i> series, be sure to give it a try. Knight was my very first KA read, and he's one of my all time favorite guys. And, there's no way you'll be able to resist Raid. Trust me on that one!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>*** ARC kindly provided to <a href="http://readinginfection.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Reading Infection</a> by Kristen Ashley &amp; Chas, in exchange for an honest review ***</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2412694558363008135" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7265887308357238823"><br/><b>barely 3 stars...<br/><br/>It doesnt look like it, concerning the actual number of pages, BUT for me, this was a loooooong fucking book...<br/><br/>it wore me the fuck out!</b><br/><br/>I might get into some ranting later...but now i m wasted and off to bed...<br/><br/>Ok, i have a love/hate relationship with KA book, and this one happened to end up on a lower scale of my mood swing...<br/><br/>Apart from the remark above...this book felt like a neverending story...and the push/pull or run/chase/catch game they play was maybe interesting the first </span>
  <span id="freeText7265887308357238823" style="display:none"><br /><b>barely 3 stars...<br /><br />It doesnt look like it, concerning the actual number of pages, BUT for me, this was a loooooong fucking book...<br /><br />it wore me the fuck out!</b><br /><br />I might get into some ranting later...but now i m wasted and off to bed...<br /><br />Ok, i have a love/hate relationship with KA book, and this one happened to end up on a lower scale of my mood swing...<br /><br />Apart from the remark above...this book felt like a neverending story...and the push/pull or run/chase/catch game they play was maybe interesting the first two times but after that i kept rolling my eyes...<br /><br />The characters...well, i usually dislike/hate the cavemanish alphas in her books but some heroes i actually do like *shrugs*<br />Anyway Raiden, the main character here...i dunno...he felt off...at times i liked him kinda but then he was more like a demanding egomaniac and "know-it-all" patronizing alpha/prick<br /><br />Example: the heroine Hanna (who was smth between a doormat and i dont know what, but they say she's sweet, cute, lovely with a big heart, lets leave it at that) wants to address Raid's past in the Marines, he snaps at her in utter rage, calls her a cunt and demands from her to leave (which she does) and they are already in a relationship!!! Than he "cools off" and comes to her house with a demanding presence saying "hey, sorry i reacted badly, lets fuck" (i'm emphasizing here) and when she asks him to leave cause he had no right to speak or treat her in such way, he just presses forward, waving it off and he does not leave, cause he knows she really doesnt want him to..and she succumbs to him again, again, again...<br /><br />The fuck was that?<br /><br />Now, that was annoying...and where's the respect in that? Huh? Up your ass...that s where...<br /><br />Ok, next on my list is a writing style!!!<br />It's a combination of intertwined descriptional sentences and short dialogues (especially when the hero is in a caveman mode, cause you know, in between the grunts and growls there are also syllables and short term words like "come here", "now"...etc.) but what actually "killed" me were sentences like this one...<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She doesn’t do it for me, Hanna, because I didn’t fall in love with her when I saw her across a street, hair shining in the sun, laughing. You do it for me because you were that girl across the street, your hair shining in the sun, laughing, making me fall in love with you, and I didn’t even goddamned fucking know you.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />See, this sausage like sentence made me cringe...with a huge WTF? question...and since i read mostly at night...this tends to either put me to sleep since i have no fuckin clue what i have just read...as i got lost somewhere in the middle of the sentence forgeting what i have read at the beginning...or DNF the book<br /><br />well, since i didnt DNF, i ended up annoyed and not on one occasion.<br /><br />See, how i also used a sausage like sentence to present my issue?! Did you get lost? I know what i m talking about...and i still get lost lol<br /><br /><b>BUT since i DID like some parts of the book i decided not to diminish it with the parts i disliked, so therefore barely 3 stars.</b><br /><br />*ranting over*<br /></span>

<div id="review_510520346" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510520346" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510520346?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510520346" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2860623270243642180"><b>PURE ROMANTIC BLISS!!! ANOTHER ABSOFUCKINGAMAZING BOOK FROM KRISTEN ASHLEY!!!!</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/5030632531_6cb899d3bb_z.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380908948i/3176627._SY540_.jpg' alt='Porch Swing photo 5030632531_6cb899d3bb_z.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>When he just stood there, his eyes moving over me, I asked softly, “Sweetheart, are you okay?” His eyes came to mine. His body slanted to the side so his shoulder was resting against the post and he replied, “You, just like that, any man would fight and die for the privilege of comin’ home to that every day.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Raiden Miller and Hanna Boudreaux both grew up in Willow, Colorado. A town so small, that m</span>
  <span id="freeText2860623270243642180" style="display:none"><b>PURE ROMANTIC BLISS!!! ANOTHER ABSOFUCKINGAMAZING BOOK FROM KRISTEN ASHLEY!!!!</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/5030632531_6cb899d3bb_z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380908948i/3176627._SY540_.jpg" alt="Porch Swing photo 5030632531_6cb899d3bb_z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>When he just stood there, his eyes moving over me, I asked softly, “Sweetheart, are you okay?” His eyes came to mine. His body slanted to the side so his shoulder was resting against the post and he replied, “You, just like that, any man would fight and die for the privilege of comin’ home to that every day.”</i>
</b><br><br>Raiden Miller and Hanna Boudreaux both grew up in Willow, Colorado. A town so small, that most everyone there knew everyone else...and that was true of these two as well...at least halfway true. Hanna saw and fell in love with Raiden Ulysses Miller when she was six years old. He was nine at the time and didn't know she existed. And that was how it remained...for years. They may have grown up side by side, but Hanna might as well have been invisible, and she knew it. <br><br>Raid was the town hunk, and would later become the town hero after returning from serving in the Marines. He had been gone for years and now he was back, and her feelings for him were still just as strong, if not more so. But he still didn't see her. He didn't recognize her. He didn't even know she existed. But this didn't deter Hanna from going into his sister's cafe, day after day, just hoping for a glimpse of him. But seeing him one day in the arms of another woman, a woman who she saw as her complete opposite, Hanna's hopes and dreams of Raiden Ulysses Miller were crushed. <br><br><b>
  <i>But she was one of those skanky skanks who looked cool. Who worked her skankedness. Who made skankdom something you’d consider aspiring to. Not to mention, her skankedness got her in a clinch with Raiden Ulysses Miller.</i>
</b><br><br>So she gave up. Moved on. Decided to start making some changes, and started living her life, taking advantage of all the things she was missing out on before.<br><br>It wasn't long after this time that Raid noticed. No. He NOTICED! And this is where their story begins. But Hanna soon finds that he may not have noticed her for the reason she thinks. But it's too late, she's already laid her heart out in the open, ready for certain destruction. <br><br><b>
  <i>"My reward."</i>
</b><br><br>This was an addicting story to read. I found myself glued to the book. It was a relatively short story, for a Kristen Ashley book. But it packed no less of her usual punch!!!! It was a heart-warming romance that I think I could read over and over. The characters were all fantastic!!!! Raid was just gorgeous. Not only was he incredibly hot, he was completely badass, sexy as hell, and the perfect alpha. He was also loving and very protective of his girl. Oh... and he likes to play...SO DAMN HOT!!!!! He did have his share of imperfections though few. He was occasionally moody and dangerous. He was dealing with a horrific past. He suffered as a soldier and was dealing with more than his share of PTSD. <br><br><b>
  <i>If you’re the kind of woman who can withstand the blaze of hellfire he’s got burning inside, he battles that and wins, you will know nothing for the rest of your life, no taste, no experience, not even the birth of your children that will be sweeter than the love he’ll have for you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Hanna was sweet and shy and a bit of a goof. I really loved her character. She was insecure in her appearance, even though she was pretty, but she also wasn't afraid to stand up for herself when she was wronged. She wasn't afraid to be herself, and instead of wallowing in self-pity, she picked herself up and made her life better!!! She was a refreshing leading lady, and it was a joy to be in her head.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/I-Love-my-Bicycle.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380908948i/3176628._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo I-Love-my-Bicycle.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I also just loved Miss Mildred, Hanna's great grandmother. I loved Hanna and Raid's devotion to her. I loved her spunky style and her fabulous in your face advice! I also loved Hanna's best friend KC, and her no nonsense view of love and romance, as well as her attitude toward her own jackass husband!!<br><br>And then there was Spot...what an awesome addition to the story...that funny fat cat!!!!<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Animals/laban-09-05-21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380908948i/3176629.jpg" alt=" photo laban-09-05-21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>...need I say more.<br><br>The quotes in this book were just fabulous...and let me tell you, that Raid is a talker! He had so much to say at times I couldn't even keep up with him. He may not have shared his mind with many people, but he sure shared it with Hanna...which I LOVED!!! He was never afraid to say what he was thinking. And he also wasn't afraid to let her know how he felt about her. WOW...HOW REFRESHING!!!! Finally a hot badass alpha that actually knows how to communicate!!!! I'm definitely in LOVE!!!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>week. You think I’m a man who’s got a thing that good, he’ll let it go?” “No,” I whispered. “That would be fuck no,” he corrected. Holy Moses.</i>
</b><br><br>I highly recommend this book... as I do ALL Kristen Ashley books. She is truly a romantic genius!!! The only thing I think I could say bad about this book, was that it was too short. Other than that...PERFECTION!!!<br><br><b>5 HEART-MELTING STARS</b><br><br><b>Raiden Ulysses Miller</b> (as cast by Aestas!)<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/99AC927C-C391-4DEF-8C88-71D9256B2529-6313-0000088982458526.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380908948i/3176630.jpg" alt="Justin Clynes photo 99AC927C-C391-4DEF-8C88-71D9256B2529-6313-0000088982458526.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Hanna Boudreaux</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/MagdaMielcarz1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380908948i/3176631.jpg" alt=" photo MagdaMielcarz1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510414945?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510414945" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8409657481246456349"><b>
  <i>”You get home in one piece, she’s your reward.” His body pressed into mine and his face, partly shadowed, came to within an inch of mine. “You’re my reward, Hanna.”<br/>My reward.<br/>Oh.<br/>My.<br/>God.</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405760i/790935._SX540_.jpg' width='379' height='325' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I loved Raiden Miller and Hanna Boudreaux, they were a great couple KA style!! <br/><br/>From the very first chapter where we find Hanna stalking Raiden at the coffee shop, I was hooked and totally on board for this hot, sweet and sexy tale! <br/><br/>Hanna Boudreaux is our Peggy Sue type character and well Raiden is hot, alpha, t</span>
  <span id="freeText8409657481246456349" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”You get home in one piece, she’s your reward.” His body pressed into mine and his face, partly shadowed, came to within an inch of mine. “You’re my reward, Hanna.”<br>My reward.<br>Oh.<br>My.<br>God.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405760i/790935._SX540_.jpg" width="379" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I loved Raiden Miller and Hanna Boudreaux, they were a great couple KA style!! <br><br>From the very first chapter where we find Hanna stalking Raiden at the coffee shop, I was hooked and totally on board for this hot, sweet and sexy tale! <br><br>Hanna Boudreaux is our Peggy Sue type character and well Raiden is hot, alpha, tortured and totally stalking worthy. She has been crushing Raiden since she was six years old. Sadly he doesn’t notice her until years later but when he does...Raiden holds nothing back with his feelings or in the bedroom.<br><br>I thoroughly enjoyed this book, as well as the cameos from our past heroes. The business mixed with Hanna and Raiden’s love story made for a great read.<br><br>I loved that porch swing, that fat cat and of course Gramma!!<br><br><b>
  <i>”Proud of you, son. You do things others can’t do and you stay standing. Now get upstairs and reap your rewards.”~Gramma</i>
</b><br><br>I had an idea for the next book in the Unfinished Hero Series: <br><br>Nick Sebring gets caught up in some crazy stuff. He falls for an undercover heroine who is FBI or some sort of law. I think Nick actually falling for someone would make for a great read and he is a bit of an ass so a fun read. <br><br>Forever a KA fan!! <br></span>

<div id="review_1766035824" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1766035824" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1766035824?book_show_action=true">Oct 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1766035824" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6197265537502157436"><b>*** 3.49 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with my best buds at BB&B!!! Yes, we are still addicted to KA, it is an addiction - we cannot help it! </b><br/><br/><i> "... “Raiden is a silly-@ss romance novel hero’s name my Mom came up with to torture me,” he replied. <br/><br/>I stifled a giggle and remarked, “And Raid isn’t silly?” <br/><br/>He smiled. “Raid’s a bad@ss’s name.”..."</i><br/><br/>Another KA book, another super-alpha male!!! This one is a GI Joe with PTSD and a tendency not to notice plain looking good girls. So, this ex GI, Raiden Miller, has been b</span>
  <span id="freeText6197265537502157436" style="display:none"><b>*** 3.49 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with my best buds at BB&amp;B!!! Yes, we are still addicted to KA, it is an addiction - we cannot help it! </b><br /><br /><i> "... “Raiden is a silly-@ss romance novel hero’s name my Mom came up with to torture me,” he replied. <br /><br />I stifled a giggle and remarked, “And Raid isn’t silly?” <br /><br />He smiled. “Raid’s a bad@ss’s name.”..."</i><br /><br />Another KA book, another super-alpha male!!! This one is a GI Joe with PTSD and a tendency not to notice plain looking good girls. So, this ex GI, Raiden Miller, has been back home from a tour "over there" for several months and spends several evenings a week at the office of his sisters' diner. This is the main reason Hanna Boudreaux, a long-legged but otherwise unremarkable nice girl, has been frequenting the establishment exactly those evenings, drinking coffee and having some good food, but mostly hoping that one day Raiden will notice her. She has been mooning over him since she was 8 years old and her crush has been classified more like a crush on a celebrity or a movie actor - completely unrealistic and unreachable. But one evening, before going into the office, he had given her a chin-lift for hello, and Hanna has been drinking coffee with a small spark of hope ever since. Until she saw him making out with a flashy, trashy, big-haired and large-breasted, definitely noticeable chick in the parking-lot, and Hanna comes to some difficult decisions. <br /><br />I have to admit, I hated that she had to change her appearance, her stile of dress and life, get some designer shoes and clothes, a fast car and a pink bike, mostly in order to be noticed. Yes, she claimed it is so she would stop living in the pages of a book and have some actual living done, but it sucks that she made those choices only when she saw that she might be too plain and boring for Raiden. Lucky for her, the ruse worked and the hot ex-soldier noticed, looked her over, and decided to move in on the chick who looked like she could star in a rom-com. After bumping into her in a pat food store, he shows up at her granny's house and he proceeds with a siege on her person. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>" ... “Coulda knocked me over with a feather, the front bell went and I opened the door to that tall drink of cool water. Woke up and I knew it was a good day. Felt it in my bones. Opened the door to him, glad I was right.” ..."</i>
</b><br /><br />As always, KA gives us a ton of wonderful secondary characters and the grandma and the cat were my favorite. The sexy times were hot, the flirting adorable. The plot was still less than substantial, but as long as you accept that this is a romance novel and it is all about the two lovebirds, you can cope with the barely existing mystery. KA is great with characterization and relationships, but her plots are usually as thin as the paper they are written on. At least, this time the alpha male had more than 50 word vocabulary and was kind of adorable in combination with the good girl gone naughty love interest. There is also the usual angst and drama typical for her romances, but no explosions, kidnappings or shootouts, which was a bit of a letdown... With all of its flaws, this book was still very pleasant to read and gives me hope that KA has more in her magic pen for the future:) <br /><br /><i>"... “Am I gonna traumatize the fat cat if he sees me fuckin' you?"<br />"As you know, his name is Spot, and he's immune to trauma. You can't feel it if your life is devoted to dishing it out.”..."</i><br /><br />This book can be read as a stand-alone, as could all the books in this series. They are all romances with a bit of a dark thread to them, usually a consequence of some trauma in the past they have not truly dealt with. The language is pure KA - pedestrian and a bit crass at times, but somehow OK the way she does it. KA fans would mostly enjoy it, I would think:)<br /><br />I wish all of you Happy Reading and may your favorite authors never disappoint you!!! <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6197265537502157436" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_548175068" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="KatLynne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne"><img alt="KatLynne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296698899p2/2435483.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548175068?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KatLynne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KatLynne" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne">KatLynne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=smokin-hot-steamy">smokin-hot-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-alpha-warrior">hero-alpha-warrior</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=one-of-my-favorite-series">one-of-my-favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=g-contemporary-romance">g-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=small-town-livin">small-town-livin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=sweet-warm-romance">sweet-warm-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-gunslinger-or-bounty-hunter">hero-gunslinger-or-bounty-hunter</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548175068" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer440164538613570937"><b>Raiden Ulysses Miller</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1256.beta.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Couples/ADDEDTOPHOTOBUCKED_zps1938d9d6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787003i/490321.jpg' alt=' photo ADDEDTOPHOTOBUCKED_zps1938d9d6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>“If you’re the kind of woman who can withstand the blaze of hellfire he’s got burning inside, he battles that and wins, you will know nothing for the rest of your life, no taste, no experience, not even the birth of your children that will be sweeter than the love he’ll have for you.” </b> <br/><br/>Kristen Ashley feeds my addiction for possessive, protective, gorgeous alpha males. With Ex-Marine <i>Raiden Ulysses Miller</i> she does it very well! He’s intense, confident, arrogant, bossy and</span>
  <span id="freeText440164538613570937" style="display:none"><b>Raiden Ulysses Miller</b><br><br><a href="http://s1256.beta.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Couples/ADDEDTOPHOTOBUCKED_zps1938d9d6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379787003i/490321.jpg" alt=" photo ADDEDTOPHOTOBUCKED_zps1938d9d6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“If you’re the kind of woman who can withstand the blaze of hellfire he’s got burning inside, he battles that and wins, you will know nothing for the rest of your life, no taste, no experience, not even the birth of your children that will be sweeter than the love he’ll have for you.” </b> <br><br>Kristen Ashley feeds my addiction for possessive, protective, gorgeous alpha males. With Ex-Marine <i>Raiden Ulysses Miller</i> she does it very well! He’s intense, confident, arrogant, bossy and I loved all six feet four inches of his broad, muscular self! <br><br>Raid’s life hasn’t been easy. Beginning early in childhood, he had to deal with a sleazebag dad. At eighteen he joined the Marines thinking to make this a career. His last deployment changed all that. It was a horror story unfolding that left unimaginable grief in its wake. Now he’s fighting demons and white knuckling the effects of PTSD. He’s back in his hometown of Willow, Colorado, a war hero doing a job many would classify as criminal activity. While his alpha-ness may never let him admit it, this tough fighter is also in need of some TLC. <br><br>And who better to surround him in all that he deserves than the lovely, sweet Hanna Boudreaux. She’s smart, kind, with just enough quirkiness to make her adorable and real. She’s lived her whole life in this small town surrounded by friends and family. She’s had a crush on Raid since she was six years old. Now that he’s back, she’s hoping he’ll finally <i>‘see’ </i>her. And when she finally comes under his radar, she’s left with the big question, why? <i>Why now, after all these years, is Raiden Ulysses Miller interested in the quiet, somewhat shy Hanna?</i><br><br>KA has given another winning installment in her <i>Unfinished Hero</i> series. She drew me in and not only did I want Hanna to get the man of her dreams, but I needed Raid to find a resting place for his heart. It’s smokin’ hot and includes one of the most loveable secondary characters I’ve read. Hanna’s ninety-eight year old g-grandmother, Miss Mildred, easily steals the limelight in many scenes. I was quite taken by her and the memories she evoked of my own precious grandmother was heartwarming. <br><br>There were a few things I missed in this book. One was the conflict/drama between the H/h that I look to KA for. It usually packs a punch and keeps me anxiously turning the pages. It did present itself early on, but was quickly resolved. I wished for more. I also felt the character development wasn’t as deeply fleshed as in her previous books. Saying that, I still devoured this one. But, when comparing to her previous books, I felt something missing. <br><br>What wasn’t missing was the unique and awesome Epilogue this author gives. It’s one of the very best ever and I will be forever spoiled by her exceptional endings. <br><br><b>Raid</b> is the third installment in Kristen Ashley’s <i>Unfinished Hero</i> series. This has surprisingly turned into one of my favorite series and I’m drawn to each of the men who live by their own codes. They’re tough, bossy, OTT protective and oozing sex appeal. And yet, underneath all this dangerous testosterone are men who love deeply, protect fiercely and each have a hidden desire to be surrounded in the nurturing comforts of home and the love of their family.</span>
  <a data-text-id="440164538613570937" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer527862363" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16501820782410947231">4.5 STARS! <br/>Bravo Kristen Ashley! You never fail me! I loved this book!<br/><br/>Sweet, goofy, dorky, honest, loyal, innocent.....all describe Hanna Boudreaux. She lives alone in an old farmhouse in Willow, Co, knits afghans and cans fruit for a living. She also takes care of her wise, sweet 98 year old great grandmother Mildred. She has a car, two actually, but prefers her shiny pink bike with the cute basket and streamers on the handlebars. Most importantly, Hanna has crushed on the town's local war hero</span>
  <span id="freeText16501820782410947231" style="display:none">4.5 STARS! <br>Bravo Kristen Ashley! You never fail me! I loved this book!<br><br>Sweet, goofy, dorky, honest, loyal, innocent.....all describe Hanna Boudreaux. She lives alone in an old farmhouse in Willow, Co, knits afghans and cans fruit for a living. She also takes care of her wise, sweet 98 year old great grandmother Mildred. She has a car, two actually, but prefers her shiny pink bike with the cute basket and streamers on the handlebars. Most importantly, Hanna has crushed on the town's local war hero Raiden Ulysses Miller since she was 6 years old. She sits in Raid's sister's diner daily just to get a glimpse of him but he pays her no attention..... So eventually she gives up, focuses on her career, getting a new hairstyle, new clothing and just being happy. What she doesn't notice is Raid now notices HER..... With her ridiculous pink bike, matching outfit and goofy, captivating innocence. Her awesome hair and long legs don't hurt....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/d80715120f4bd8c102e28d82cfa14f53_zps79df7477.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408359i/798812.jpg" alt=" photo d80715120f4bd8c102e28d82cfa14f53_zps79df7477.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>All badass, emotionally scarred war hero. He returns to Willow, leaving the Marines to assist Knight Sebring in some undercover "business." A huge chunk of him died when his comrades were killed and he will never heal from that. He's just going about life....until he sets eyes on this cute little brunette with the goofy ass bike talking across the street to the local pothead bike store owner. He's got to meet her....he can't take his eyes off her.<br><br>My Raid...<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Male%20Eye%20Candy/b4706a1e824e6a55890e79f83d37c80a_zps3a8f49e7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408359i/798813._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo b4706a1e824e6a55890e79f83d37c80a_zps3a8f49e7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I loved loved loved Hanna. She was so innocent and funny...KA pulled her character off flawlessly. Enter badass, foul-mouthed Raid and it's just comical. He's as tough and worldly as she is soft and clueless, I loved the qualities in Hanna that drew such a guy to her but also her ability to not judge him and to do what she could to help Raid battle the demons that haunt him.<br><br>My Hannah.....<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps807462c3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408359i/798814.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps807462c3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Grandma Mildred.....oh, we'd all love a spunky, wise one like her. She loved her granddaughter but also knew a man like Raiden Miller would love and protect her to his dying day. Her cat- Spot! I loved that crotchety obese feline!<br><br>Meet Spot...<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zpsf4cbce1f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408359i/798815.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsf4cbce1f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The book flowed well, the chemistry awesome, the plot well developed. My only issue is probably the length being a bit short for Kristen Ashley. The story of the drug dealers could've been drawn out in more detail (as would've typically been done in most of her other books). I'm used to a kind of (sometimes crime) mystery with most KA books and this was present but took a huge minor backseat in the story- kind of skimmed over it, I guess.<br><br>Anyways, I loved it. Loved Hanna, loved Raid, loved GGM Mildred, Spot...... Bravo!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16501820782410947231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548685982?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17258026-raid">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548685982" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5468728859454645163">I cannot believe I am only giving 3 stars to a KA book. I think the problem is that us KA addicts have been totally spoiled by her previous books.They are so much longer than Raid, have much more detail in them. I did like it but it could have been so much more. We never really got inside Raid's head ... what did happen with his army buddies - yeah they were blown to smithereens but i wanted to read more about his reactions and mental state. Hanna was lovely but I missed any shopping she might h</span>
  <span id="freeText5468728859454645163" style="display:none">I cannot believe I am only giving 3 stars to a KA book. I think the problem is that us KA addicts have been totally spoiled by her previous books.They are so much longer than Raid, have much more detail in them. I did like it but it could have been so much more. We never really got inside Raid's head ... what did happen with his army buddies - yeah they were blown to smithereens but i wanted to read more about his reactions and mental state. Hanna was lovely but I missed any shopping she might have done, even more descriptions about her clothes and jewelry - as I said we have been spoiled by previous books. Some have commented about the sameness to other books - I did not mind that as that is one of the reasons I like KA is because her books can have the same theme and writing style running through them. Was I the only person who was dying to find out he got the name Ulysses? Maybe that is the Irish in me and the fact that my now husband was very impressed when I told him, on our first date, that I had read Ulysses ... I haven't and he says that can now be grounds for divorce as that was the only reason he married me!! He was an English Lit student at the time. But that is beside the point - I would recommend the book but just wish it had left me with the usually happy glow that I have when I have finished any other book by Ms. Ashley.Then again don't think any hero is going to live up to the expectation of my first true love, Tate Jackson.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5468728859454645163" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w0BH9bYNRcq8vWTOqQEsJs6Xp9lvRXyuEixowXxG33P4/95IQUCXsxMDG+VQAmPw01sVO4/QA5GEWyJkjMsg+Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('B9/DgvYyNlaGysjqr7N8C69p1rkxQiztGY4B8+sd2i88YFo/AX/kLyl0t8FWsDPdsqVkW9HXU9KP+UtWG5AlpQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer7955880152244494661">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText7955880152244494661" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
